  .linkify {
    display: inline;

  a:hover, .linkify:hover {

  }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }

          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





The navigate-to CSP directive is currently marked as "in development"; see 



<span class="line"><!---->The navigate-to CSP directive is currently marked as "in development"; see <!----></span>





https://chromestatus.com/feature/6457580339593216



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromestatus.com/feature/6457580339593216"><!---->https://chromestatus.com/feature/6457580339593216<!----></a>





.



<span class="line"><!---->.<!----></span>





 Prakash Sharma (please CC him: 



<span class="line"><!----> Prakash Sharma (please CC him: <!----></span>





prakash0x00@gmail.com



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/prakash0x00@gmail.com"><!---->prakash0x00@gmail.com<!----></a>





) and I noticed that it's implemented on the Dev channel in such a way that it blocks (with a CSP error) a redirect (in a redirect chain, possibly) if the target of that redirect is not listed as a source in that directive.



<span class="line"><!---->) and I noticed that it's implemented on the Dev channel in such a way that it blocks (with a CSP error) a redirect (in a redirect chain, possibly) if the target of that redirect is not listed as a source in that directive.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This behaviour seems to contradict the spec (see 



<span class="line"><!---->This behaviour seems to contradict the spec (see <!----></span>





https://www.w3.org/TR/CSP3/#directive-navigate-to



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://www.w3.org/TR/CSP3/#directive-navigate-to"><!---->https://www.w3.org/TR/CSP3/#directive-navigate-to<!----></a>





),



<span class="line"><!---->),<!----></span>





 if our interpretation of it is correct:



<span class="line"><!----> if our interpretation of it is correct:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    The navigate-to directive restricts the URLs to which a document can initiate navigations by any means (a, form, window.location, window.open, etc.). This is an enforcement on what navigations this document initiates not on what this document is allowed to navigate to.



<span class="line"><!---->    The navigate-to directive restricts the URLs to which a document can initiate navigations by any means (a, form, window.location, window.open, etc.). This is an enforcement on what navigations this document initiates not on what this document is allowed to navigate to.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In any case, this behaviour opens the door to XSLeaks (partial bypass of the SOP), because the document that initiated the navigation can observe that the latter led to a redirect to a target not listed in its navigate-to directive.



<span class="line"><!---->In any case, this behaviour opens the door to XSLeaks (partial bypass of the SOP), because the document that initiated the navigation can observe that the latter led to a redirect to a target not listed in its navigate-to directive.<!----></span>



<br>





This behaviour is reminiscent of the behaviour currently exhibited by the form-action directive, which I've shown to be problematic in 



<span class="line"><!---->This behaviour is reminiscent of the behaviour currently exhibited by the form-action directive, which I've shown to be problematic in <!----></span>





https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1259077



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1259077"><!---->https://bugs.chromium.org/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1259077<!----></a>



<br>



<br>

<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>

<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Linux<!----></span>

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
